***побежать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:побежать.html>побежа́ть</a> (1124)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побежать.html>побежа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobežátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start running, to break into a run</li>
<li>to begin to flow <i>(about liquids)</i></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">Bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побежать.html>побежа́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">pobežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b> are concrete verbs. Their counterpart, <b><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></b>, is an abstract verb.
</p>

</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 5b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:побеждать.html>побежда́ть</a> (8168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pobedítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побеждать.html>побежда́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pobeždátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:победить.html>победи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to win, to be victorious over, to conquer, to vanquish, to defeat</li>
<li>to overcome</li>
<li>to beat</li></ol>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>блёк<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ший <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бле́к<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ший</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:действительный.html>Действи́тельное</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поблагодарить.html>поблагодари́ть</a> (5144)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blagodarítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поблагодарить.html>поблагодари́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poblagodarítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:благодарить.html>благодари́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to thank
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поблагодарить.html>поблагодари́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жена.html>жену́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:обед.html>обе́д</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вкусный.html>вку́сно</a>!</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Poblagodarí</b> ženú za obéd, óčenʹ vkúsno!</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Thank</b> (your) wife for the dinner, (it was) very delicious!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>бла<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>го<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:да.html>да</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ри́ть</b>

***поблескивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:поблескивать.html>побле́скивать</a> (5610)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:получать.html>по-</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">po-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">блеск-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blesk-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Apparently formed from an underlying root <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">блеск-</span> of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блестеть.html>блесте́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blestétʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:блеск.html>блеск</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">blesk</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">brilliance, luster</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:поболтать.html>поболта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poboltátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to chat (have a chat) <i>(with about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поболтать.html>поболта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:немного.html>немно́го</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poboltátʹ</b> nemnógo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a chat; chat(ter) a little</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:поболтать.html>поболта́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:полчаса.html>полчаса́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>poboltátʹ</b> polčasá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a half-hour's chat; chat for half an hour</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:побороться.html>поборо́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">poborótʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бороться.html>боро́ться</a></b>)
